# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/navidrome--9c3b4561` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/navidrome--9c3b4561$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Write Integration Tests for Navidrome Media Scanner

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/navidrome--9c3b4561 (mirror of navidrome/navidrome)
**Output:** Write your test file to `/workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Navidrome's media scanning pipeline. Navidrome scans a music library directory, extracts metadata from audio files, and persists track/album/artist records to a database.

## Scope

Explore the scanner package (`scanner/`) and its dependencies. Key areas:
- `scanner/scanner.go` — top-level scanner entry point
- `scanner/metadata/` — audio file metadata extraction
- `core/artwork/` — artwork extraction
- Database persistence via the store interfaces

Your integration tests must cover:
- Full scan of a test fixture directory with mock audio files
- Metadata extraction (title, artist, album, year, track number)
- Album and artist record creation
- Incremental scan (re-scan with no changes produces no DB updates)
- File deletion detection (missing file removes DB record)

## Output Format

Write a Go test file at:
```
/workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go
```

Use Go's `testing` package. Each test function must start with `Test`. Use test fixtures (small audio files or mock file system) where needed.

## Quality Bar

- At least 5 test functions
- Cover at least 3 pipeline stages (file discovery, metadata extraction, DB persistence)
- Include at least one negative case (deleted file, corrupt metadata)
- Do not fabricate package names or function signatures — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

## Summary of Integration Tests Written

I've created `/workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go` with **7 test functions** covering the scanner pipeline:

### Test Functions

1. **TestFullScanOfFixtureDirectory** - Tests the complete scan pipeline with real audio files from `tests/fixtures`
   - Verifies changes are detected
   - Confirms media files are persisted to the database
   - Validates metadata extraction

   - Title extraction (from tags or filename)
   - Suffix extraction (file extension)
   - LibraryID assignment
   - Timestamp tracking

3. **TestAlbumAndArtistCreation** - Tests album and artist record creation during scan
   - Verifies album/artist records are created with proper IDs
   - Checks LibraryID is set correctly
   - Validates record structure integrity

4. **TestIncrementalScanWithNoChanges** - Tests re-scan behavior without file modifications
   - Performs initial scan
   - Sets LastScanAt timestamp
   - Verifies second scan detects no changes
   - Confirms file count remains consistent

5. **TestFileDeletionDetection** - Tests deletion detection (negative case)
   - Pre-populates DB with fake deleted files
   - Scans empty folder
   - Verifies deleted files are removed from DB

6. **TestCorruptMetadataHandling** - Tests scanner resilience (negative case)
   - Scans `tests/fixtures/invalid-files` with corrupt metadata
   - Verifies scanner completes without panicking
   - Tests error handling with invalid files

1. WRITE /workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go
package scanner

import (
	"context"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/google/uuid"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/core/artwork"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/log"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/model"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/tests"
)

// TestFullScanOfFixtureDirectory tests the complete scan pipeline with real audio files
func TestFullScanOfFixtureDirectory(t *testing.T) {
	ctx := context.Background()

	// Create mock repositories
	mfRepo := tests.CreateMockMediaFileRepo()
	albumRepo := tests.CreateMockAlbumRepo()
	artistRepo := tests.CreateMockArtistRepo()
	genreRepo := &tests.MockedGenreRepo{}

	ds := &tests.MockDataStore{
		MockedMediaFile: mfRepo,
		MockedAlbum:     albumRepo,
		MockedArtist:    artistRepo,
		MockedGenre:     genreRepo,
	}

	// Create scanner with mock datastore and empty playlists/cacheWarmer
	scanner := NewTagScanner(ds, &mockPlaylists{}, &mockCacheWarmer{})

	// Create a test library pointing to the fixtures directory
	lib := model.Library{
		ID:         1,
		Name:       "Test Library",
		Path:       "tests/fixtures",
		LastScanAt: time.Time{}, // First scan
	}

	// Run the scan
	progress := make(chan uint32, 100)
	changeCount, err := scanner.Scan(ctx, lib, false, progress)
	close(progress)

	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Scan failed: %v", err)
	}

	// Verify that changes were detected
	if changeCount == 0 {
		t.Errorf("Expected changes to be detected, but got changeCount=0")
	}

	// Verify that media files were added to the database
	allFiles, err := mfRepo.GetAll()
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Failed to get all media files: %v", err)
	}

	if len(allFiles) == 0 {

// ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo extends MockMediaFileRepo with scanner-required methods
type ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo struct {
	*tests.MockMediaFileRepo
	paths map[string]struct{}
}

func NewExtendedMockMediaFileRepo() *ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo {
	return &ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo{
		MockMediaFileRepo: tests.CreateMockMediaFileRepo(),
		paths:             make(map[string]struct{}),
	}
}

func (m *ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo) Put(mf *model.MediaFile) error {
	if mf.Path != "" {
		m.paths[mf.Path] = struct{}{}
	}
	return m.MockMediaFileRepo.Put(mf)
}

func (m *ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo) FindPathsRecursively(basePath string) ([]string, error) {
	// Return all paths that start with basePath
	var result []string
	for path := range m.paths {
		if strings.HasPrefix(path, basePath) {
			result = append(result, filepath.Dir(path))
		}
	}
	return result, nil
}

func (m *ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo) FindAllByPath(path string) (model.MediaFiles, error) {
	var result model.MediaFiles
	all, _ := m.MockMediaFileRepo.GetAll()
	for _, mf := range all {
		if strings.HasPrefix(mf.Path, path) {
			result = append(result, mf)
		}
	}
	return result, nil
}

func (m *ExtendedMockMediaFileRepo) FindByPath(path string) (*model.MediaFile, error) {
	all, _ := m.MockMediaFileRepo.GetAll()
	for _, mf := range a
... (truncated)
